[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 7bb3f9683ba8f59b[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security vulnerability has been detected in the Apache Commons Compress [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary's `Expander` class. The fuzzer has identified a file path traversal [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m22[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where the code attempts to access a file path outside the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp7590114066078088114/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepresents a security issue that could potentially allow an attacker to write files[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto arbitrary locations on the filesystem.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception thrown by Jazzer's[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity sanitizer, specifically the `FilePathTraversal` detection mechanism. This [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates that during the expansion of an archive file, the code attempted to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreate or access a file path that traverses outside the designated output [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe exception originates from:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - The core validation method that detected the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.checkPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - Path validation logic[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - A hook that intercepts file operations[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following call chain:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - Entry point where fuzzer provides test [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m216[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Initial expansion method[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m336[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Intermediate expansion method[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m412[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Further expansion processing[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m502[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Point where the path traversal is attempted[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe multiple `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method calls in the stack trace suggest the code handles [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested or recursive archive expansion scenarios.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Attempted Path**: The system attempted to access [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp7590114066078088114/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`, which appears [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto be outside the intended extraction directory based on the security check [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailure.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Vulnerability Type**: This is a classic path traversal vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39malso [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mknown as directory traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where malicious archive entries could potentially [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite files outside the intended destination directory.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Detection Point**: The vulnerability was caught at line [0m[1;36m502[0m[39m in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.java`, indicating this is where file operations occur that could be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexploited.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this security issue, the following [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` class**:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m502[0m[39m: The exact location where the path traversal occurs[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m216[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m336[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m412[0m[39m: The expansion method chain to understand the flow[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Path validation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor lack thereof[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before file operations[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How archive entry names are processed and resolved to filesystem paths[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Archive Entry Processing**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How entry names from archives [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZIP, TAR, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are extracted and used[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether entry names containing [0m[32m".."[0m[39m or absolute paths are sanitized[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The logic that constructs output file paths from entry names[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Input Data Analysis**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The specific archive structure that triggered this vulnerability[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malicious entry names that could exploit this weakness[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Controls**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current path validation mechanisms in place [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Output directory boundary enforcement[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Canonicalization of paths before file operations[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis vulnerability represents a critical security flaw as it could allow malicious [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive files to write arbitrary files to the filesystem, potentially leading to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode execution, data exfiltration, or system compromise.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add helper method to read symlink target**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd a new private method to read symlink target content:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate <T extends ArchiveEntry> byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m[1;35mreadSymlinkTarget[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T>[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriter, T entry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new [0m[1;35mByteArrayOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry, baos[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;35mbaos.toByteArray[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Remove the vulnerable [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method**[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: lines [0m[1;36m508[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m524[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This method is no longer needed and is the source of the vulnerability[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete the entire method[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Security Improvements[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Symlink Location Validation**: The symlink file location is validated via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m, ensuring it's within bounds[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Symlink Target Validation**: The symlink target path is separately validated [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure it also resolves within the target directory bounds[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Unsafe Symlink Following**: Unlike `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, we never [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollow existing symlinks when creating parent directories - we use [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which handles this safely[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Atomic Validation**: All path validation happens BEFORE any filesystem [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectory creation or symlink creation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Consistent Pattern**: All archive types now use the same secure expansion [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Handling Edge Cases[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Relative Symlink Targets**: The validation using [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtargetDirPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msymlinkTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` correctly handles both relative [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"../dir"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and absolute paths[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Symlink Already Exists**: The check `![0m[1;35mFiles.isRegularFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents overwriting existing symlinks or files[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Null Target Directory**: The existing null checks handle the case where [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction happens to NullOutputStream[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Cross-Platform**: The symlink handling is conditional on `[0m[1;35misUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturning true, so it only affects Unix-style archives[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserving Existing Functionality[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility**: The `testSymLinks` test [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m294[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will continue to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwork because:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symlinks are still created in the filesystem[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symlink targets are still resolved[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Files can still be written to symlink-resolved paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas long as they're [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin bounds[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Path Traversal Tests**: All existing security tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m191[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m218[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will pass [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecause:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` validates entry names[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symlink targets are also validated[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both validations happen before filesystem operations[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **API Compatibility**: The public API of `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods remains unchanged[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Root Cause**: Removes the vulnerable `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod that followed symlinks without validation[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Validates both symlink locations AND symlink targets[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent Security**: All archive types use the same secure pattern[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Features**: Symlink support is preserved but made secure[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Code Simplification**: Reduces overall code complexity by removing the custom [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mZipFile implementation[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Proven Pattern**: Uses the existing `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method which is documented [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand tested for zip slip prevention[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Consideration[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf modifying the generic expand method is deemed too risky [0m[1;39m([0m[39maffecting all archive [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, an alternative minimal fix would be to:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Keep the [0m[1;35mZipFile.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m custom implementation[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add validation in `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` after line [0m[1;36m516[0m[39m:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.isSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    current = [0m[1;35mFiles.readSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate the resolved path is still within root[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcurrent.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mroot.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Symlink escapes target directory: "[0m[39m + current[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Add validation at lines [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m481[0m[39m for symlink targets before creating them[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, this alternative is **NOT recommended** because it:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains the inconsistent pattern across archive types[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keeps complex, hard-to-audit code[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- May miss other edge cases in the custom implementation[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe refactoring approach is strongly preferred for long-term security and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintainability.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.j[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mav[0m[1;92ma:96[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m105[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
